### [409] [Structural Parameters for Steiner Orientation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21445)
*Tesshu Hanaka,Michael Lampis,Nikolaos Melissinos,Edouard Nemery,Hirotaka Ono,Manolis Vasilakis*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: Steiner Orientation 问题在树宽等参数下是 NP 完全的，其顶点覆盖数参数化的算法是 $n^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$ 且最优。该问题在 $|A|$ 参数下有 $2^{\mathcal{O}(|A|)}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法，并且在 $\mathrm{tw}+k$、距离团和 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 参数下是 FPT 的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究的动机在于理解 Steiner Orientation 问题的结构参数复杂性。该问题要求在混合图中定向无向边，使得指定的源汇对之间存在有向路径。研究者希望通过研究该问题对于不同参数（如树宽、顶点覆盖数等）的复杂性，来揭示其内在的计算难度。

Method: 本研究采用结构参数复杂性的视角，研究了 Steiner Orientation 问题的复杂性。具体研究了以下几个方面：1. 在反馈顶点数（feedback vertex number）为 2、树宽（treewidth）为 2、路径宽（pathwidth）为 3 和顶点完整性（vertex integrity）为 6 的实例上，证明了 Steiner Orientation 问题的 NP 完全性。2. 提出了一个参数化为顶点覆盖数 $\mathrm{vc}$ 的 XP 算法，其时间复杂度为 $n^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$，并证明了该算法的运行时间在本质上是最优的（否则将与 ETH 冲突）。3. 分析了以无向边数量（$|E|$）或有向边数量（$|A|$）为参数的复杂性，指出对于 $|E|$ 的 $2^{|E|}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法在 SETH 下是最优的，并提出了一个针对 $|A|$ 的 $2^{\mathcal{O}(|A|)}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法。4. 探讨了问题在参数化为 $\mathrm{tw}+k$、距离团（distance to clique）和 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 时的复杂性，并证明了这些情况下问题是 FPT 的（对于 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 还有多项式核）。

Result: Steiner Orientation 问题在特定参数下（如反馈顶点数 2、树宽 2、路径宽 3、顶点完整性 6）是 NP 完全的。存在一个参数化为顶点覆盖数 $\mathrm{vc}$ 的 $n^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$ 时间 XP 算法，该算法的运行时间在本质上是最优的。对于参数 $|E|$，存在一个最优的 $2^{|E|}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法。对于参数 $|A|$，存在一个 $2^{\mathcal{O}(|A|)}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法。问题在参数 $\mathrm{tw}+k$、距离团和 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 下是 FPT 的，其中 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 参数化还有多项式核。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，Steiner Orientation 问题在结构参数复杂性方面具有挑战性。例如，在特定参数（如反馈顶点数、树宽、路径宽和顶点完整性）下，该问题是 NP 完全的。此外，研究还提出了一个关于顶点覆盖数的 XP 算法，其运行时间 $n^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$，并且证明了该运行时间在本质上是最优的，因为任何更快的运行时间（$n^{o(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$）都将与 ETH 冲突。对于边数（$|E|$ 或 $|A|$）的参数化，研究指出针对 $|E|$ 的 $2^{|E|}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法在 SETH 下是最优的，同时提出了一个针对 $|A|$ 的 $2^{\mathcal{O}(|A|)}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$ 算法。最后，研究还探讨了该问题在 $\mathrm{tw}+k$、距离团（distance to clique）和 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 等参数下的参数化复杂性，并指出这些情况下问题是 FPT 的（对于 $\mathrm{vc}+k$ 还有多项式核）。

Abstract: We consider the \textsc{Steiner Orientation} problem, where we are given as
input a mixed graph $G=(V,E,A)$ and a set of $k$ demand pairs $(s_i,t_i)$,
$i\in[k]$. The goal is to orient the undirected edges of $G$ in a way that the
resulting directed graph has a directed path from $s_i$ to $t_i$ for all
$i\in[k]$. We adopt the point of view of structural parameterized complexity
and investigate the complexity of \textsc{Steiner Orientation} for standard
measures, such as treewidth. Our results indicate that \textsc{Steiner
Orientation} is a surprisingly hard problem from this point of view. In
particular, our main contributions are the following: (1) We show that
\textsc{Steiner Orientation} is NP-complete on instances where the underlying
graph has feedback vertex number 2, treewidth 2, pathwidth 3, and vertex
integrity 6; (2) We present an XP algorithm parameterized by vertex cover
number $\mathrm{vc}$ of complexity $n^{\mathcal{O}(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$.
Furthermore, we show that this running time is essentially optimal by proving
that a running time of $n^{o(\mathrm{vc}^2)}$ would refute the ETH; (3) We
consider parameterizations by the number of undirected or directed edges ($|E|$
or $|A|$) and we observe that the trivial $2^{|E|}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$-time
algorithm for the former parameter is optimal under the SETH. Complementing
this, we show that the problem admits a
$2^{\mathcal{O}(|A|)}n^{\mathcal{O}(1)}$-time algorithm. In addition to the
above, we consider the complexity of \textsc{Steiner Orientation} parameterized
by $\mathrm{tw}+k$ (FPT), distance to clique (FPT), and $\mathrm{vc}+k$ (FPT
with a polynomial kernel).

</details>


### [410] [Online Edge Coloring: Sharp Thresholds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21560)
*Joakim Blikstad,Ola Svensson,Radu Vintan,David Wajc*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了新的在线图边着色算法，在特定条件下实现了比以往更优的着色效果，并填补了确定性算法和随机化算法性能上的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决在线图边着色问题中，确定性算法和随机化算法的性能提升问题。研究者们希望找到能够超越现有算法（如贪心算法）的着色方法，并验证在特定条件下是否可以实现接近最优的 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 着色。

Method: 本文提出了一种新的确定性在线算法，能够为最大度为 $\Delta = \omega(\log n)$ 的图实现 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的边着色。同时，还设计了一种随机化算法，在最大度 $\Delta = \omega(\sqrt{\log n})$ 时也能达到 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的着色。

Result: 本文的主要成果是提出了两种新的在线图边着色算法。第一种是确定性算法，适用于最大度 $\Delta = \omega(\log n)$ 的图，能够实现 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的着色。第二种是随机化算法，适用于最大度 $\Delta = \omega(\sqrt{\log n})$ 的图，同样能实现 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的着色。这些结果显著提升了在线图边着色算法的性能上限。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了在在线图边着色问题中，确定性算法和随机化算法的性能界限。对于最大度 $\Delta = \omega(\log n)$ 的图，我们提出了一种确定性在线算法，可以实现 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的着色。此外，对于最大度 $\Delta = \omega(\sqrt{\log n})$ 的图，我们也提出了一种随机化算法，能够达到 $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ 的着色。这些结果填补了确定性算法和随机化算法在性能上的空白，并与先前的不可能性结果相匹配。

Abstract: Vizing's theorem guarantees that every graph with maximum degree $\Delta$
admits an edge coloring using $\Delta + 1$ colors. In online settings - where
edges arrive one at a time and must be colored immediately - a simple greedy
algorithm uses at most $2\Delta - 1$ colors. Over thirty years ago, Bar-Noy,
Motwani, and Naor [IPL'92] proved that this guarantee is optimal among
deterministic algorithms when $\Delta = O(\log n)$, and among randomized
algorithms when $\Delta = O(\sqrt{\log n})$. While deterministic improvements
seemed out of reach, they conjectured that for graphs with $\Delta =
\omega(\log n)$, randomized algorithms can achieve $(1 + o(1))\Delta$ edge
coloring. This conjecture was recently resolved in the affirmative: a $(1 +
o(1))\Delta$-coloring is achievable online using randomization for all graphs
with $\Delta = \omega(\log n)$ [BSVW STOC'24].
  Our results go further, uncovering two findings not predicted by the original
conjecture. First, we give a deterministic online algorithm achieving $(1 +
o(1))\Delta$-colorings for all $\Delta = \omega(\log n)$. Second, we give a
randomized algorithm achieving $(1 + o(1))\Delta$-colorings already when
$\Delta = \omega(\sqrt{\log n})$. Our results establish sharp thresholds for
when greedy can be surpassed, and near-optimal guarantees can be achieved -
matching the impossibility results of [BNMN IPL'92], both deterministically and
randomly.

</details>


### [411] [Towards Tight Bounds for Estimating Degree Distribution in Streaming and Query Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21784)
*Arijit Bishnu,Debarshi Chanda,Gopinath Mishra*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文解决了图的互补累积度数直方图（ccdh）的近似问题，在流式和查询模型中给出了下界，并解决了子线性模型中的复杂度问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了近似图的互补累积度数直方图（ccdh），本文考虑了（εD, εR）-双标准乘法近似，该近似在域和范围中都允许受控的乘法松弛，而其精确复杂度是WOLA 2019上提出的一个悬而未决的问题。

Method: 设计了一个算法来近似ccdh，该算法独立于任何子线性模型，并表明在流式和查询模型中可以有效地获得所需的样本。

Result: 在查询和流模型中建立了ccdh近似的第一个下界，并几乎解决了该问题在子线性模型中的复杂度。

Conclusion: 该研究首次为图的互补累积度数直方图（ccdh）在查询和流模型中建立了下界，并几乎解决了该问题在子线性模型中的复杂度问题。

Abstract: The degree distribution of a graph $G=(V,E)$, $|V|=n$, $|E|=m$ is one of the
most fundamental objects of study in the analysis of graphs as it embodies
relationship among entities. In particular, an important derived distribution
from degree distribution is the complementary cumulative degree histogram
(ccdh). The ccdh is a fundamental summary of graph structure, capturing, for
each threshold $d$, the number of vertices with degree at least $d$. For
approximating ccdh, we consider the $(\varepsilon_D,\varepsilon_R)$-BiCriteria
Multiplicative Approximation, which allows for controlled multiplicative slack
in both the domain and the range. The exact complexity of the problem was not
known and had been posed as an open problem in WOLA 2019 [Sublinear.info,
Problem 98].
  In this work, we first design an algorithm that can approximate ccdh if a
suitable vertex sample and an edge sample can be obtained and thus, the
algorithm is independent of any sublinear model. Next, we show that in the
streaming and query models, these samples can be obtained efficiently. On the
other end, we establish the first lower bounds for this problem in both query
and streaming models, and (almost) settle the complexity of the problem across
both the sublinear models.

</details>

### [412] [Heterogeneous Ensemble Enables a Universal Uncertainty Metric for Atomistic Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21297)
*Kai Liu,Zixiong Wei,Wei Gao,Poulumi Dey,Marcel H. F. Sluiter,Fei Shuang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为 U 的不确定性度量，用于评估通用机器学习内原子势能 (uMLIPs) 的可靠性。基于此度量，开发了一种模型蒸馏框架，可以高效地生成特定于应用的势能，同时保证准确性，甚至在某些情况下优于原始 DFT 数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用机器学习内原子势能 (uMLIPs) 正在重塑原子模拟，但缺乏可靠、通用的不确定性量化限制了其安全广泛的应用。

Method: 该研究提出了一种基于异构模型集成和预训练 uMLIPs 重用的不确定性度量 U。利用该度量，提出了一种不确定性感知的模型蒸馏框架，以生成特定于系统的势能。

Result: U 度量显示出与真实预测误差的强相关性，并能对配置级风险进行稳健排序。基于 U 度量的蒸馏框架能够生成特定于系统的势能，在 W 的情况下，仅用 4% 的 DFT 标签即可达到与完整 DFT 训练相当的准确性；在 MoNbTaW 的情况下，无需额外 DFT 计算。过滤数值标签噪声后，蒸馏模型在某些情况下准确性甚至超过了 DFT 参考标签。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一个统一的、可扩展的不确定性度量 U，该度量基于异构模型集成和预训练的 uMLIPs 的重用。U 显示出与真实预测误差的强相关性，并提供对配置级风险的稳健排序。利用此度量，研究提出了一个不确定性感知的模型蒸馏框架，用于生成特定于系统的势能。在 W 的情况下，仅使用 4% 的 DFT 标签即可实现与完整 DFT 训练相当的准确性；对于 MoNbTaW，则无需额外的 DFT 计算。此外，通过过滤数值标签噪声，蒸馏模型在某些情况下甚至可以超越 DFT 参考标签的准确性。该不确定性感知的 U 指标为 uMLIPs 的可靠性提供了实用的监控，并指导数据选择和微调策略，从而促进了基础模型的构建和安全使用，并实现了准确、特定于系统的势能的高效开发。

Abstract: Universal machine learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) are reshaping
atomistic simulation as foundation models, delivering near \textit{ab initio}
accuracy at a fraction of the cost. Yet the lack of reliable, general
uncertainty quantification limits their safe, wide-scale use. Here we introduce
a unified, scalable uncertainty metric \(U\) based on a heterogeneous model
ensemble with reuse of pretrained uMLIPs. Across chemically and structurally
diverse datasets, \(U\) shows a strong correlation with the true prediction
errors and provides a robust ranking of configuration-level risk. Leveraging
this metric, we propose an uncertainty-aware model distillation framework to
produce system-specific potentials: for W, an accuracy comparable to full-DFT
training is achieved using only \(4\%\) of the DFT labels; for MoNbTaW, no
additional DFT calculations are required. Notably, by filtering numerical label
noise, the distilled models can, in some cases, surpass the accuracy of the DFT
reference labels. The uncertainty-aware approach offers a practical monitor of
uMLIP reliability in deployment, and guides data selection and fine-tuning
strategies, thereby advancing the construction and safe use of foundation
models and enabling cost-efficient development of accurate, system-specific
potentials.

### [413] [Investigating the effects of local environment on nitrogen vacancies in high entropy metal nitrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21362)
*Charith R. DeSilva,Matthew D. Witman,Dallas R. Trinkle*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高熵金属氮化物中氮空位形成能的影响因素，以建立一个预测模型，理解其稳定性和力学性质。

Method: 使用密度泛函理论计算了六种不同的高熵氮化物中氮空位的形成能，并构建了一个预测模型。通过最大化氮原子环境的超胞和计算氮位点的能量密度，发现了能量密度与空位形成能之间的相关性，并基于最近邻组成建立了线性回归模型。

Result: 建立了预测氮空位形成能的模型，发现能量密度与空位形成能相关，并确定了不同金属对空位形成能的影响顺序（Hf > Zr > Ti > V > Cr > Ta > Nb > Mo）。同时指出，仅使用二元氮化物数据不足以预测高熵氮化物的复杂行为。

Conclusion: 高熵金属氮化物的氮空位形成能与氮原子位点的能量密度相关，并且可以使用基于最近邻组成的线性回归模型进行预测。该模型对高熵氮化物具有预测性和可解释性，并与实验数据一致。

Abstract: High entropy metal nitrides are an important material class in a variety of
applications, and the role of nitrogen vacancies is of great importance for
understanding their stability and mechanical properties. We study six different
high entropy nitrides with eight different metal species to build a predictive
model of the nitrogen vacancy formation energy. We construct sets of supercells
that maximize the number of unique nitrogen environments for a given chemistry,
and then use density-functional theory to calculate the energy density for all
nitrogen sites, and the vacancy formation energies for the highest, lowest, and
a median subset based on the energy densities. The energy density of nitrogen
sites correlates with the vacancy formation energies, for binary, ternary and
high entropy nitrides. A linear regression model predicts the vacancy formation
energies using only the nearest-neighbor composition; across our eight metals,
we find the largest vacancy formation energies next to Hf, then Zr, Ti, V, Cr,
Ta, Nb, and the lowest near Mo. Additionally, we see that binary nitride data
shows qualitatively similar vacancy formation energy trends for high entropy
nitrides; however, the binary data alone is insufficient to predict the complex
nitride behavior. Our model is both predictive and easily interpretable, and
correlates with experimental data.

characteristics can be tuned via a perpendicular electric field and electron
doping. Our findings offer a new concept for the development of fully
graphene-based spintronic devices utilizing the three distinct electronic
phases of rhombohedral trilayer graphene.

Abstract: With a swift progress in modern high-throughput communication systems,

the central wavelength. Similarly, the rGOLC film reaches 50 % absorption with
a 1.68 micrometer thickness, 279 times smaller than the central wavelength.
These findings provide valuable insights for development of GO- and rGO-based
LC THz absorbers with highly tunable properties due to the ordering of GO
flakes. Specifically, the LC phase of GO contributes to the formation of more
uniform films with enhanced absorption due to the compact stacking and denser
packing, compared to conventional GO films with randomly oriented GO flakes.

### [417] [Theoretical investigations of the origin of persistent luminescence in spinel oxides MgGa2O4 and MgAl2O4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21599)
*Xiuli Yang,Ran Zhou,Hongliang Shi,Yifeng Duan,Mao-Hua Du*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过混合泛函计算，研究揭示了 MgGa2O4 和 MgAl2O4 的持久发光机制，确定了关键的缺陷及其在发光过程中的作用，并为实验结果提供了理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MgGa2O4 和 MgAl2O4 因其独特的固有持久发光而备受关注，在各种应用中具有广阔的应用潜力。

Method: 采用精确的混合泛函计算，从缺陷物理学的角度系统地研究了 MgGa2O4 和 MgAl2O4 中持久发光现象的起源。

Result: 研究确定了两种材料中的主要点缺陷是涉及两种阳离子的空位和反位缺陷。MgGa 缺陷的光激发和发射峰与 MgGa2O4 中实验观察到的 2.9 eV 蓝光发射峰吻合良好。在 MgAl2O4 中，VO-MgAl 供体-受体缺陷复合物内的内部缺陷光跃迁被确定为观察到的 2.7 eV 发射峰的可能起源。计算出的 MgGa 和 VO-MgAl 的辐射复合系数远高于非辐射系数，这支持了它们作为有效发光中心的地位。此外，计算出的氧空位 VO 在 MgGa2O4 和 MgAl2O4 中的光学过程与实验结果一致，计算出的陷阱深度也与热释光光谱测量结果一致。

Conclusion: MgGa2O4 和 MgAl2O4 的固有持久发光源于电子陷阱（MgGa 和 VO）和空穴陷阱（MgAl）。此外，MgGa2O4 中的供体-受体缺陷复合物（VO+VMg 和 VO+VGa）也是有效的载流子陷阱中心。

Abstract: MgGa2O4 and MgAl2O4 have attracted significant interest due to their unique
intrinsic persistent luminescence, offering promising potential for various
applications. In this paper, from the perspective of defect physics, we
systemically investigate the origin of persistent luminescence phenomena in
pristine MgGa2O4 and MgAl2O4, employing accurate hybrid functional
calculations. Our results show that vacancies and antisite defects involving
the two cations are the dominant point defects in both materials. Our
calculated optical excitation and emission peaks associated with the MgGa
defect agree well with the experimentally observed blue luminescence peak at
about 2.9 eV in MgGa2O4. In MgAl2O4, the intradefect optical transition within
the VO-MgAl donor-acceptor defect complex is identified as a likely origin for
the observed 2.7 eV emission peak. Furthermore, the calculated radiative
recombination coefficients of MgGa and VO-MgAl are significantly higher than
their nonradiative counterparts, supporting their roles as efficient
luminescent centers. Our results regarding the optical processes of oxygen
vacancy VO in MgGa2O4 and MgAl2O4 are also in good agreement with experimental
results. Based on the calculated defect thermodynamic transition levels, the
intrinsic persistent luminescence in MgGa2O4 and MgAl2O4 may be attributed to
electron traps, GaMg and VO, in the former and a hole trap, MgAl, in the
latter. Donor-acceptor defect complexes (VO+VMg and VO+VGa) are also found to
serve as effective carrier trapping centers in MgGa2O4. The calculated trap
depths are also consistent with thermoluminescence spectroscopy measurements.

</details>

### [419] [Ultralow Lattice Thermal Conductivity Induced by Quasi-Chain Configuration in Rb2Se3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21634)
*Tiantian Jia,Yongsen Tang,Yongsheng Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: Rb2Se3具有极低的晶格热导率（<0.2 W/mK），这源于其独特的准链状结构，结合了刚性的Se三聚体和软性的Rb离子骨架，导致了强烈的声子非谐性和 the rattling-like behavior。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碱金属化合物因其极低的晶格热导率在热电能量转换和热障涂层领域具有重要应用潜力，但其根本机制尚不明确。因此，本研究旨在探究Rb2Se3中极低晶格热导率的内在起源。

Method: 本研究利用第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）结合声子玻尔兹曼输运方程（BTE），揭示了Rb2Se3中极低晶格热导率的内在机制。

Result: 研究表明，Rb2Se3在300 K时沿所有晶向的晶格热导率低于0.2 W/mK。这主要是由于其独特的准链状结构，其中刚性的Se-Se-Se三聚体与Rb原子形成的弱相互作用的间隙位点相结合，产生了显著的各向异性、弱键合、强非谐性和普遍存在的 the rattling-like behavior，从而导致低频声子模式占主导地位。

Conclusion: Rb2Se3具有低于0.2 W/mK的晶格热导率，这归因于其独特的准链状结构，其中包含刚性的Se-Se-Se三聚体和较弱键合的Rb原子。这种结构导致了明显的各向异性、弱键合、强非谐性和显著的 the rattling-like behavior，所有这些因素共同作用，极大地抑制了声子传导，为设计具有低晶格热导率的材料提供了新思路。

Abstract: Alkali metal-based compounds have garnered significant attention due to their
exceptionally low lattice thermal conductivity, which is crucial for
applications in thermoelectric energy conversion and thermal barrier coatings.
However, the fundamental mechanisms underlying such ultralow lattice thermal
conductivity remain poorly understood. In this study, we investigate the
intrinsic origins of the ultralow lattice thermal conductivity in the alkali
metal-based ionic compound Rb2Se3, which exhibits a simple orthorhombic
structure. By employing first-principles density functional theory (DFT) and
solving the phonon Boltzmann transport equation (BTE), we reveal that Rb2Se3
achieves lattice thermal conductivity values below 0.2 W/mK along all
crystallographic directions at 300 K. Our analysis uncovers a unique
quasi-chain configuration within the crystal structure, characterized by
strongly covalent Se-Se-Se trimers that act as localized rigid units, while Rb
atoms occupy weakly bonded interstitial sites. This configuration induces
pronounced anisotropy, weak bonding, and strong anharmonicity, leading to
significant rattling-like behavior of all atoms and a dominance of
low-frequency phonon modes. The interplay between the rigid Se trimers and the
soft Rb matrix results in extreme phonon anharmonicity, as evidenced by large
Gruneisen parameters and high atomic displacement parameters (ADPs). These
findings provide a comprehensive understanding of the low lattice thermal
conductivity in Rb2Se3 and establish a universal framework for designing low
lattice thermal conductivity materials through the combination of rigid
covalent clusters and soft ionic sublattices.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究通过实验研究了两种pnictides（砷和铋）的磁场驱动金属-绝缘体转变（MIT）。通过低至10K的温度和高达14T的磁场测量了Shubnikov de Haas（SdH）振荡和巨磁阻（MR）。此外，还基于微观模型对观察到的现象进行了理论解释。

Result: 研究发现，在低温下，铋表现出在强磁场下重entrantIMT的异常行为，以及在较小磁场下温度较高的MIT。砷则表现出典型的单MIT。两种材料在10K以下均表现出二维电子气（2DEG）行为。在2K和14T的横向磁场下，观察到高达10^5%的巨磁阻。

Abstract: The metal to insulator (MIT) transition is accompanied with huge changes in
physical responses by the control and tuning of experimental parameters like
doping, pressure, chemical composition, and magnetic field. Here, we study the
magnetic field driven MIT for two pnictides in their elemental form, namely
Arsenic and Bismuth. At low temperatures, Bismuth shows an unusual behaviour of

smaller fields. However, Arsenic shows the commonly observed single MIT. The
Shubnikov de Haas (SdH) oscillations are observed for both As and Bi below 10
K, elucidating their two-dimensional electron gas (2DEG) behaviour at low
temperatures. Giant magneto-resistance of the order of 10^5 percent (MR

field. Based on a microscopic model, the microscopic processes underpinning the
unusual features of a field-driven MIT and re-entrant IMT, along with the

excitonic condensate and Das-Doniach preformed pair scenarios in one single

### [421] [Dielectric Properties of Single Crystal Calcium Tungstate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21662)
*Elrina Hartman,Michael E Tobar,Ben T McAllister,Jeremy F Bourhill,Andreas Erb,Maxim Goryachev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: Microwave WGM analysis of CaWO$_4$ revealed its dielectric properties and loss mechanisms from room temperature to 4 K. Permittivity values were measured, with the perpendicular component being 4.8% lower than literature. Loss tangents improved by two orders of magnitude at cryogenic temperatures but were higher than expected, possibly due to spin interactions. Findings suggest WGM utility for sensing in quantum systems and cryogenic detectors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To characterize the dielectric properties and loss mechanisms of single-crystal calcium tungstate (CaWO$_4$) using microwave whispering gallery mode (WGM) analysis, particularly across a wide temperature range from room temperature down to cryogenic conditions, and to explore the potential of this technique for probing lattice dynamics and enabling novel sensing applications.

Method: Microwave whispering gallery mode (WGM) analysis was utilized to measure the dielectric properties (relative permittivity and loss tangent) of a cylindrical, single-crystal CaWO$_4$ sample across a temperature range from 295 K down to 4 K. Both quasi-transverse-magnetic (QTM) and quasi-transverse-electric (QTE) mode families were analyzed to assess loss mechanisms and determine the biaxial permittivity components ($\epsilon_{||}$ and $\epsilon_{\perp}$) relative to the crystal

Result: The study reports biaxial permittivity values for CaWO$_4$ at 295 K as $\epsilon_{||} = 9.029 \pm 0.09$ and $\epsilon_{\perp} = 10.761 \pm 0.11$, and at 4 K as $\epsilon_{||} = 8.797 \pm 0.088$ and $\epsilon_{\perp} = 10.442 \pm 0.104$. The parallel component agreed with literature, but the perpendicular component was found to be 4.8% lower. Loss tangents at 295 K were measured as $\tan\delta_{||}^{295,\mathrm{K}} = (4.1 \pm 1.4) \times 10^{-5}$ and $\tan\delta_{\perp}^{295,\mathrm{K}} = (3.64 \pm 0.92) \times 10^{-5}$. Upon cooling to 4 K, loss tangents improved significantly to $\tan\delta_{||}^{4,\mathrm{K}} = (1.56 \pm 0.52) \times 10^{-7}$ and $\tan\delta_{\perp}^{4,\mathrm{K}} = (2.05 \pm 0.79) \times 10^{-7}$. The cryogenic loss tangents were higher than previous reports, possibly due to an unidentified paramagnetic spin ensemble.

Conclusion: The investigation successfully employed microwave WGM analysis to characterize the dielectric properties of CaWO$_4$ from room temperature to cryogenic conditions. The WGM technique demonstrated high precision, with measured dielectric constants and loss tangents agreeing with literature values where available, while also revealing discrepancies that may be attributed to previously unobserved loss mechanisms at cryogenic temperatures, potentially related to paramagnetic spin ensembles. These findings underscore the utility of WGMs for material characterization and sensing applications, particularly in the context of quantum systems and cryogenic detectors.

Abstract: This investigation employed microwave whispering gallery mode (WGM) analysis
to characterize the dielectric properties of a cylindrical, single-crystal
sample of calcium tungstate (CaWO$_4$). Through investigation of
quasi-transverse\hyp{}magnetic and quasi-transverse\hyp{}electric mode
families, we can assess loss mechanisms and relative permittivity from room
temperature down to cryogenic conditions. We report the biaxial permittivity
values of $\epsilon_{||} = 9.029 \pm 0.09$ and $\epsilon_{\perp} = 10.761 \pm
0.11$ at $295$ K, and $\epsilon_{||} = 8.797 \pm 0.088$ and $\epsilon_{\perp} =
10.442 \pm 0.104$ at $4$ K. Components are denoted with respect to the
c\hyp{}axis of the crystal unit cell. The parallel component agrees well with
the published literature at MHz frequencies; however, the perpendicular
component is $4.8$\% lower. The WGM technique offers greater precision, with
accuracy limited primarily by the uncertainty in the crystal's dimensions. WGMs
also serve as sensitive probes of lattice dynamics, enabling monitoring of
temperature-dependent loss mechanisms. At room temperature, the measured loss
tangents were $\tan\delta_{||}^{295,\mathrm{K}} = (4.1 \pm 1.4) \times 10^{-5}$
and $\tan\delta_{\perp}^{295,\mathrm{K}} = (3.64 \pm 0.92) \times 10^{-5}$.
Upon cooling to 4 K, the loss tangents improved by approximately two orders of
magnitude, reaching $\tan\delta_{||}^{4,\mathrm{K}} = (1.56 \pm 0.52) \times
10^{-7}$ and $\tan\delta_{\perp}^{4,\mathrm{K}} = (2.05 \pm 0.79) \times
10^{-7}$. These cryogenic values are higher than those reported in prior
studies, likely due to a magnetic loss channel associated with an unidentified
paramagnetic spin ensemble. These findings have implications for the use of
CaWO$_4$ in applications such as spin-based quantum systems and cryogenic
bolometry, highlighting the potential of WGMs for novel sensing applications.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this study, we systematically investigate the thermal and electronic
transport properties of two-dimensional PbSe/PbTe monolayer heterostructure by
combining first-principles calculations, Boltzmann transport theory, and
machine learning methods. The heterostructure exhibits a unique honeycomb-like
corrugated and asymmetric configuration, which significantly enhances phonon
scattering. Moreover, the relatively weak interatomic interactions in PbSe/PbTe
lead to the formation of anti-bonding states, resulting in strong anharmonicity
and ultimately yielding ultralow lattice thermal conductivity (${\kappa_{\rm
L}}$). In the four-phonon scattering model, the ${\kappa_{\rm L}}$~values along
the $x$ and $y$ directions are as low as 0.37 and 0.31 W/mK, respectively.
Contrary to the conventional view that long mean free path acoustic phonons
dominate heat transport, we find that optical phonons contribute approximately
59\% of the lattice thermal conductivity in this heterostructure. These optical
phonons exhibit large Gr\"uneisen parameters, strong anharmonic scattering, and
relatively high group velocities, thereby playing a crucial role in the low
${\kappa_{\rm L}}$ regime. Further analysis of thermoelectric performance shows
that at a high temperature of 800 K, the heterostructure achieves an
exceptional dimensionless figure of merit ($ZT$) of 5.3 along the $y$
direction, indicating outstanding thermoelectric conversion efficiency. These
findings not only provide theoretical insights into the transport mechanisms of
PbSe/PbTe monolayer heterostructure but also offer a practical design strategy
for developing high-performance two-dimensional layered thermoelectric
materials.

### [425] [Electrochemically-driven formation of Intermetallic Cu3ZnLi2 alters Li-transport in nanostructured bimetallic battery anode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21673)
*Eric V. Woods,Xinren Chen,Yuwei Zhang,J. Manoj Prabhakar,Patricia Jovičević-Klug,Matic Jovičević-Klug,Mahander P. Singh,Yujun Zhao,Siyuan Zhang,Stefan Zaefferer,Jian Liu,Yug Joshi,Baptiste Gault*

TL;DR: 纳米晶黄铜集流体在锂金属电池循环中会形成三元Laves相，导致容量损失。研究提出了微结构演化机制，并建议评估二元合金集流体在不同循环条件下的相形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锂基电池的运行寿命常因枝晶的形成而受限，而纳米晶双金属集流体可用于阳极无锂电池，改善锂沉积并抑制枝晶形成。本研究旨在探究黄铜集流体的微结构演化及其对锂金属电池性能的影响。

Method: 通过电化学循环和显微结构分析，研究了黄铜集流体（Cu 63% Zn 37%）在无阳极锂金属电池中的微结构演化过程，并提出了包括动态重结晶和相形成在内的演化机制。

Result: 研究发现，在100次循环后，黄铜集流体初始的纳米晶变形层部分转化为三元Laves相Cu3ZnLi2，同时伴随着纳米晶黄铜基体的生长。锂剥离过程中，该相部分分解，但剩余部分会螯合锂，形成“死锂”，导致容量损失。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种微结构演化机制，包括动态重结晶和相形成，解释了在锂金属电池循环过程中黄铜集流体上三元Laves相的形成。由于该三元Laves相是在电化学循环中形成的，因此需要评估二元合金集流体在不同循环条件下的亚稳三元相形成，以稳定和利用这些相或完全电化学剥离它们。

Abstract: The role of Li-based batteries in the electrification of society cannot be
understated, however their operational lifetime is often limited by the
formation of dendrites, i.e. the localised deposition of Li that can cause
shorts between the two electrodes leading to the failure of the battery.
Nanocrystalline bimetallic current collectors can be used for anode-free
Li-metal batteries, with improved Li plating and limited or suppressed
formation of dendrites. Here, we demonstrate that the microstructure of an
alpha-Brass current collector, Cu 63% Zn 37%, used in an anode-free Li-metal
battery evolves during cycling. It initially had a nanocrystalline deformation
layer approximately 80 nm in thickness after polishing. After 100 cycles, the
initial deformed brass layer was partially converted to a ternary Laves phase
Cu3ZnLi2 within a nanocrystalline brass matrix that grew to 200 - 250 nm in
thickness. Upon Li stripping, the phase partially decomposes electrochemically,
but what remains can sequester Li thus forming "dead Li" thereby contributing
to capacity loss. We propose a mechanism for the microstructural evolution
including dynamic recrystallization and phase formation. Since this ternary
Laves phase emerges during electrochemical cycling alone, binary alloy current
collectors must be assessed for metastable ternary phase formation under
different cycling conditions to either stabilize and exploit such phases or
electrochemically fully strip them.

### [426] [Magnetization switching by current in an elemental ferromagnetic single layer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22016)

Abstract: Current-induced magnetization switching, a fundamental phenomenon related to

### [427] [Multiferroicity and 180$^\circ$ domain switching in LaFeO$_3$ via Antisite Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21681)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有共存且耦合的铁电和磁性材料

Method: 使用密度泛函理论计算

Abstract: Materials with coexisting and coupled ferroelectric and magnetic orders are
rare. Here we show, using density functional theory calculations, that inducing
Fe$_\mathrm{La}$ antisites into non-ferroelectric and antiferromagnetic

ferrimagnetic. Even more excitingly, we observe a direct coupling between the
ferroelectric and ferrimagnetic polarization, the latter being switchable by
the former. While on average the magnetic moments of antisites would cancel, we
envision that preparing defective LaFeO$_3$ under simultaneous electric and
magnetic fields will lead to a net magnetic moment due to magnetic domain
reconfiguration. Moreover, ferroelectric switching under a static magnetic
field can lead to 180$^\circ$ switching of the antiferromagnetic order in
LaFeO$_3$.

### [428] [Orbital-selective charge transfer drives two-step negative thermal expansion structural transitions in PbTa2Se4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21700)
*Peng Li,Xiaohui Yang,Wenhua Song,Zhefeng Lou,Tongrui Li,Zhengtai Liu,Zhu'an Xu,Zhuoyu Chen,Xiao Lin,Yang Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: PbTa2Se4中的负热膨胀由轨道选择性电荷转移驱动，且受压力调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究电荷和轨道自由度在负热膨胀效应中的作用，特别是PbTa2Se4中两步负热膨胀结构相变。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱和第一性原理计算，阐明了PbTa2Se4中异常的两步负热膨胀结构相变中的电荷和轨道动力学。

Result: 研究发现，在第一相变中，电荷主要从Pb 6pz轨道转移到费米能级以下的M形带，几乎不改变费米面；在第二相变中，费米面和电荷转移轨道均发生改变，电荷从Pb 6px/py轨道选择性地转移到Ta 5dz2轨道，由Pb 6px/py轨道形成的费米泡减小。此外，小的压力即可调控三种相的基本结构及其超导性。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了轨道选择性电荷转移驱动了PbTa2Se4中不同寻常的结构转变，为理解负热膨胀机制提供了新的见解，并为了解此类金属插入过渡金属硫族化物中调控的超导性提供了独特的窗口。

Abstract: The negative thermal expansion (NTE) effect has been found generally combined
with structural phase transitions. However, the charge and orbital freedoms of
the NTE has not been well studied. This study employs angle-resolved
photoemission spectroscopy and first-principles calculations to elucidate the
charge and orbital kinetics of the anomalous two-step negative thermal
expansion structural phase transitions in PbTa2Se4. As the temperature
decreases, each transition undergoes a similar block-layer sliding, although
the charge transfer behaviors differ significantly. During the first
transition, charge is mainly transferred from the Pb 6pz orbital to an M-shaped
band below the Fermi level, barely altering the Fermi surface. In contrast, the
second transition involves modifications to both the Fermi surface and
charge-transfer orbitals, with charge selectively transferred from Pb 6px/py
orbitals to Ta 5dz2 orbitals and a decrease of the Fermi pockets formed by Pb
6px/py orbitals. Furthermore, a small pressure can easily tune the base
structure phase among the three phases and the corresponding superconductivity.
Therefore, our findings reveal that the orbital-selective charge transfer
drives the unusual structure transition in PbTa2Se4, offering new insights into
the NTE mechanisms and providing a unique window to study the pressure-tuned
superconductivity in this metal-intercalated transition chalcogenides.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了扩展非相对论磁 ريا-chiral splitting现象到相对论能区，并探索其在先进磁 ريا器件中的应用潜力。

Method: 通过研究具有Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用的双层反铁磁体，识别了三种由特定对称性（如$C_4T$，$\sigma_v T$或其组合）决定的磁 ريا-chiral splitting类别。

Result: 发现了由三波混频介导的、扩展到相对论能区的磁 ريا-chiral splitting现象，并确定了三种不同的、由对称性保护的磁 ريا-chiral splitting类别。

Abstract: Nonrelativistic magnon chiral splitting in altermagnets has garnered
significant recent attention. In this work, we demonstrate that nonlinear

into unprecedented relativistic regimes. Employing a bilayer antiferromagnet
with Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions, we identify three distinct classes of

$\sigma_v T$, or their combination. This reveals a novel bosonic mechanism for
symmetry-protected chiral splitting, capitalizing on the unique ability of
magnons to violate particle-number conservation, a feature absent in low-energy
fermionic systems. Our findings pave the way for engineering altermagnetic
splitting, with potential applications in advanced magnonic devices and deeper
insights into magnon dynamics in complex magnetic systems.

### [430] [Investigating CO Adsorption on Cu(111) and Rh(111) Surfaces Using Machine Learning Exchange-Correlation Functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21789)
*Xinyuan Liang,Renxi Liu,Mohan Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: DeePKS机器学习方法在模拟CO与过渡金属表面相互作用时，实现了高精度（媲美HSE06）和低计算成本，解决了长期存在的“CO吸附难题”，并为催化剂设计提供了通用模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决广义梯度近似（GGA）在密度泛函理论中无法准确预测CO在过渡金属表面优先吸附在顶位这一“CO吸附难题”，并克服混合泛函（如HSE06）计算成本高昂的限制。

Method: 采用深度Kohn-Sham（DeePKS）方法训练机器学习交换-关联泛函，并利用主成分分析来选择电子结构描述符，以应对CO吸附在过渡金属表面的计算挑战。

Result: DeePKS模型成功恢复了实验上观察到的CO在Cu(111)和Rh(111)表面的吸附位点偏好，吸附能差与HSE06相当（约10 meV）。一个单一的DeePKS模型能够准确预测不同过渡金属表面的吸附能、位点偏好、势能面和吸附结构。

Conclusion: 该研究通过训练DeePKS模型，成功地以较低的计算成本实现了与混合泛函相当的精度，解决了CO吸附在过渡金属表面的“难题”，并为开发通用模型以加速催化剂探索提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: The "CO adsorption puzzle", a persistent failure of utilizing generalized
gradient approximations (GGA) in density functional theory to replicate CO's
experimental preference for top-site adsorption on transition-metal surfaces,
remains a critical barrier in surface chemistry. While hybrid functionals such
as HSE06 partially resolve this discrepancy, their prohibitive computational
cost limits broader applications. We tackle this issue by adopting the Deep
Kohn-Sham (DeePKS) method to train machine-learned exchange-correlation
functionals. Principal component analysis reveals that the input descriptors
for electronic structures separate distinctly across different chemical
environments, enabling the DeePKS models to generalize to multi-element
systems. We train system-specific DeePKS models for transition-metal surfaces
Cu(111) and Rh(111). These models successfully recover experimental site
preferences, yielding adsorption energy differences of about 10 meV compared to
HSE06. Furthermore, a single model for the two surfaces is trained, and the
model achieves comparable accuracy in predicting not only adsorption energies
and site preference but also potential energy surfaces and relaxed surface
adsorption structures. The above work demonstrates a promising path towards
universal models, enabling catalyst exploration with hybrid functional accuracy
at substantially reduced cost.

### [432] [Reducing Data Requirements for Sequence-Property Prediction in Copolymer Compatibilizers via Deep Neural Network Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21902)
*Md Mushfiqul Islam,Nishat N. Labiba,Lawrence O. Hall,David S. Simmons*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 人工智能策略加速序列控制聚合物設計。通過「預訓練和微調」深度神經網絡，利用少量數據即可在不同條件下實現高保真預測，特別適用於聚合物回收等應用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成序列控制聚合物在模仿生物蛋白質的精確序列功能方面具有巨大潛力，但其設計過程因缺乏類似蛋白質的大規模演化數據集而面臨巨大挑戰。本研究旨在開發一種人工智能策略，以顯著減少設計這些材料所需數據量，從而加速其設計進程，特別是在聚合物回收等應用中。

Method: 本研究提出了一種人工智能策略，利用深度神經網絡處理序列控制聚合物的數據。該策略的核心是「預訓練和微調」方法，即在較低的數據保真度和特定條件下訓練模型，然後利用少量數據對模型進行微調，以適應不同的預測條件和更高的保真度。

Result: 研究表明，一個在低保真數據和單一條件下訓練的深度神經網絡，能夠通過微調快速適應不同的預測條件，並提供高保真度的預測。這大大減少了傳統方法所需的數據量，證明了「預訓練和微調」方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了一種人工智能策略，利用深度神經網絡，通過「預訓練和微調」的方法，僅需少量數據即可顯著加速序列控制聚合物的設計和預測。該方法能夠將在單一條件下訓練的低保真模型快速調整到另一組條件，實現高保真預測，這對於需要針對不同條件進行設計的應用（如混合廢物聚合物回收）至關重要。

Abstract: Synthetic sequence-controlled polymers promise to transform polymer science
by combining the chemical versatility of synthetic polymers with the precise
sequence-mediated functionality of biological proteins. However, design of
these materials has proven extraordinarily challenging, because they lack the
massive datasets of closely related evolved molecules that accelerate design of
proteins. Here we report on a new Artifical Intelligence strategy to
dramatically reduce the amount of data necessary to accelerate these materials'
design. We focus on data connecting the repeat-unit-sequence of a
\emph{compatibilizer} molecule to its ability to reduce the interfacial tension
between distinct polymer domains. The optimal sequence of these molecules,
which are essential for applications such as mixed-waste polymer recycling,
depends strongly on variables such as concentration and chemical details of the
polymer. With current methods, this would demand an entirely distinct dataset
to enable design at each condition. Here we show that a deep neural network
trained on low-fidelity data for sequence/interfacial tension relations at one
set of conditions can be rapidly tuned to make higher-fidelity predictions at a
distinct set of conditions, requiring far less data that would ordinarily be
needed. This priming-and-tuning approach should allow a single low-fidelity
parent dataset to dramatically accelerate prediction and design in an entire
constellation of related systems. In the long run, it may also provide an
approach to bootstrapping quantitative atomistic design with AI insights from
fast, coarse simulations.

### [433] [Laser-Synthesized Amorphous PdSe$_{\mathrm{2-x}}$ Nanoparticles: A Defect-Rich Platform for High-Efficiency SERS, Photocatalysis, and Photothermal Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.21918)
*Andrei Ushkov,Nadezhda Belozerova,Dmitriy Dyubo,Ilya Martynov,Alexander Syuy,Daniil Tselikov,Georgy Ermolaev,Sergey V. Bazhenov,Roman I. Romanov,Ivan Kruglov,Anton A. Popov,Alexander Chernov,Alexey D. Bolshakov,Sergey Novikov,Andrey A. Vyshnevyy,Aleksey Arsenin,Andrei V. Kabashin,Gleb I. Tselikov,Valentyn Volkov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过飞秒激光烧蚀，将 PdSe$_{2}$ 转化为非晶纳米粒子，实现了优于晶体前体的拉曼散射、光催化和光热转换性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属硫族化物（TMDCs）具有显著的电子和光学性质，但其功能主要由其稳定的晶体相决定。控制原子尺度的材料性质是材料科学中的一个核心挑战。

Method: 使用无配体、单步飞秒激光烧蚀技术在液体中将结晶的、化学计量的二硒化钯（PdSe$_{2}$）转化为高度稳定、无定形的、非化学计量的纳米粒子（PdSe$_{2-x}$，其中 x$	ext{ ≈ }$1）。

Result: 这种激光诱导的非晶化产生了高密度的硒空位和配位不饱和位点，从而实现了比前体晶体 PdSe$_{2}$ 更优越的性能，例如：超过 $10^6$ 倍增强的无等离激元表面增强拉曼散射，光催化活性增加了 50 倍，近红外光热转换效率达到 83%。

Conclusion: 这项研究证明了激光诱导非晶化是一种强大的方法，可以用于缺陷工程化的过渡金属硫族化物，并推动它们在光学、催化和纳米医学中的实际应用。

Abstract: The control of material properties at the atomic scale remains a central
challenge in materials science. Transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) offer
remarkable electronic and optical properties, but their functionality is
largely dictated by their stable crystalline phases. Here we demonstrate a
single-step, ligand-free strategy using femtosecond laser ablation in liquid to
transform crystalline, stoichiometric palladium diselenide
(PdSe$_{\mathrm{2}}$) into highly stable, amorphous, and non-stoichiometric
nanoparticles (PdSe$_{\mathrm{2-x}}$, with x$\approx$1). This laser-driven

unsaturated sites, which unlock a range of emergent functions absent in the
crystalline precursor, including plasmon-free surface-enhanced Raman scattering
with an enhancement factor exceeding 10$^\mathrm{6}$, a 50-fold increase in
photocatalytic activity, and near-infrared photothermal conversion efficiency
reaching 83$\%$. Our findings establish laser-induced amorphization as a
powerful top-down approach for defect-engineered TMDCs and advances their
practical usage in optics, catalysis, and nanomedicine.

</details>
